<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клич.html>клич</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">klič</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клич.html>кли́ча</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клич.html>кли́чи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клич.html>кли́чей</a></b>)

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клоака.html>клоа́ка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">kloáka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клоака.html>клоа́ки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клоака.html>клоа́ки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клоака.html>клоа́к</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>cesspool, sink, sewer</li>
<li>foul place</li>
<li>cloaca</li></ol>

***клок.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:клок.html>клок</a> (5084)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клок.html>клок</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">klok</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клок.html>клока́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клок.html>кло́чья</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клок.html>клоки́</a><sup>*</sup></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клок.html>кло́чьев</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клок.html>клоко́в</a><sup>*</sup></b>) <span class="ib-brac"><span class="qualifier-brac">(</span></span><span class="ib-content"><span class="qualifier-content">* Meaning <i>tuft</i>, <i>flock</i> only.</span></span><span class="ib-brac"><span class="qualifier-brac">)</span></span>
</p>
<ol><li>tuft, flock</li>
<li>(plural only "<a href = vnd.unilang:клок.html>кло́чья</a>") shred, rag, tatter</li></ol>

***клокотать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:клокотать.html>клокота́ть</a> (12638)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*klokotati</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клокотать.html>клокота́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">klokotátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to bubble, to boil
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>него́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:клокотать.html>клокота́ло</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:горло.html>го́рле</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">u nevó <b>klokotálo</b> v górle</i> ― <span class="e-translation">there was a gurgle in his throat</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(emotions)</i> to boil
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>нём</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:клокотать.html>клоко́чет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:гнев.html>гнев</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v njóm <b>klokóčet</b> gnev</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he is seething with rage</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">всклокота́ть</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">vsklokotátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***клонить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:клонить.html>клони́ть</a> (13396)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*kloniti</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клонить.html>клони́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">klonítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to incline, to bend
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:лодка.html>ло́дку</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:клонить.html>кло́нит</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бок.html>бок</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">lódku <b>klónit</b> na bok</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the boat is heeling/listing</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to drive <i>(at)</i>, to get <i>(at)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:куда.html>куда́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>ты</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:клонить.html>кло́нишь</a></b>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kudá ty <b>klónišʹ</b>?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">what are you driving/getting at?</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:клонить.html>кло́нит</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ко.html>ко</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сон.html>сну</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">jevó <b>klónit</b> ko snu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he is sleepy</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***клониться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:клониться.html>клони́ться</a> (13987)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клонить.html>клони́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">klonítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клониться.html>клони́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">klonítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to bow, to bend</li>
<li>to tend <i>(to)</i>, to be aimed <i>(at)</i></li>
<li>to come close
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дело.html>де́ло</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:клониться.html>кло́нится</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:развязка.html>развя́зке</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">délo <b>klónitsja</b> k razvjázke</i> ― <span class="e-translation">matters are moving towards a solution</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:солнце.html>со́лнце</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:клониться.html>клони́лось</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:закат.html>зака́ту</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sólnce <b>klonílosʹ</b> k zakátu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the sun was setting</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>день</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:клониться.html>кло́нится</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вечер.html>вечеру</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">denʹ <b>klónitsja</b> k večeru</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the day is declining waning; evening is approaching</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клонить.html>клони́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">klonítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***клоун.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:клоун.html>кло́ун</a> (8622)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">clown</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клоун.html>кло́ун</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">klóun</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клоун.html>кло́уна</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клоун.html>кло́уны</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клоун.html>кло́унов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>clown
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">Вааг <a href = vnd.unilang:бояться.html>бои́тся</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:клоун.html>кло́унов</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Vaag boítsja <b>klóunov</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Vahag is scared of clowns.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> irresponsible person, who states unfounded claims, often  thoughtless or careless</li></ol>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">кло́унский</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">klóunskij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***клуб.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:клуб.html>клуб</a> (1164)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">клубъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">klubŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*klǫbъ</i>; cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk"><a href = vnd.unilang:клуб.html>клуб</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">klub</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">kloub</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Polish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Polish language">Polish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="pl">kłąb</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клуб.html>клуб</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">klub</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клуб.html>клу́ба</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клуб.html>клубы́</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клуб.html>клу́бы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клуб.html>клубо́в</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клуб.html>клу́бов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>cloud, puff <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of smoke, etc.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>a dense swarm <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of insects or other animals</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> lump, ball</li></ol>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Klub</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">club</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клуб.html>клуб</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">klub</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клуб.html>клу́ба</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клуб.html>клу́бы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клуб.html>клу́бов</a></b>)
</p>

***клубиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:клубиться.html>клуби́ться</a> (9291)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">клуби́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">klubítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клубиться.html>клуби́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">klubítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to curl, to wreathe, to swirl
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:дым.html>Дым</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:клубиться.html>клуби́лся</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:труба.html>трубы́</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Dym <b>klubílsja</b> iz trubý.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The chimney was belching out smoke.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пыль.html>Пыль</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:клубиться.html>клуби́тся</a></b>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Pylʹ <b>klubítsja</b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">The dust is swirling.</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">клуби́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">klubítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:клубника.html>клубни́ка</a> (17458)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клубень.html>клу́бень</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">klúbenʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tuber</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клубника.html>клубни́ка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">klubníka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клубника.html>клубни́ки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клубника.html>клубни́ки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клубника.html>клубни́к</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клубничный.html>клубни́чный</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">клубни́чка</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>strawberry (<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/garden_strawberry" class="extiw" title="w:garden strawberry">garden strawberry</a> <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Fragaria_%C3%97_ananassa" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Fragaria × ananassa"><i>Fragaria</i> × <i>ananassa</i></a></span>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/green_strawberry" class="extiw" title="w:green strawberry">green strawberry</a> <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Fragaria_viridis" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Fragaria viridis"><i>Fragaria viridis</i></a></span>, or <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/musk_strawberry" class="extiw" title="w:musk strawberry">musk strawberry</a> <span class="biota"><a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Fragaria_moschata" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Fragaria moschata"><i>Fragaria moschata</i></a></span>)</li></ol>

***клык.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:клык.html>клык</a> (7384)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*kъlykъ</i>. Cognate to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:колоть.html>коло́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kolótʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клык.html>клык</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">klyk</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клык.html>клыка́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клык.html>клыки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:клык.html>клыко́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>canine tooth</li>
<li>fang</li>
<li>tusk</li></ol>

***ключ.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ключ.html>ключ</a> (1048)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*kľučь</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*kle(h₂)uk-</i>, whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">clef</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">close</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ключ.html>ключ</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ključ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ключ.html>ключа́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ключ.html>ключи́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ключ.html>ключе́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>key</li>
<li>wrench, spanner, screw wrench</li>
<li>clue, key</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">music</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> clef, key</li>
<li>radical <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in Chinese characters</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:ключевой.html>ключева́я</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:фигура.html>фигу́ра</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ključevája</b> figúra</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>key</b> figure (as in an important person)</span></div></dd>

<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">А ведь день был особенным, <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">ключевым</span> для всего столетовского дела! </span> <span class="example-fullblock"></li>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">Приобретение лицензий на важные изобретения, решающие <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">ключевые</span> технические проблемы, часто позволяет сэкономить время и средства. </span></li>

<ol><li>связанный, соотносящийся по значению с существительным ключ никовый <span class="example-fullblock"><ul>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">Девственные чащи черемух и черешен пугливо протянули свои корни в <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">ключевой</span> холод и изредка лепечут листьями, будто сердясь и негодуя, когда прекрасный ветреник ― ночной ветер, подкравшись мгновенно, целует их. </span> <span class="example-fullblock"></li>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">Кусок черствого хлеба да <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">ключевая</span> вода ― вот и вся еда… </span> <span class="example-fullblock"></li>
<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">Мы ехали в горы, ехали с гор, проезжали чистые <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;">ключевые</span> речки, ехали черемуховой аллеей. </span></li>
</ul></li>


</ol>

***ключик.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ключик.html>клю́чик</a> (7411)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ключ.html>ключ</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ključ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ик</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
